# Results Report for *Survey on Performance Management* - Combined Questions (All Responses)

## \[C9a\] - \[C9b\] - \[C9c\]

\[C9a\]: I would trust monitoring data from monitoring tools.

\[C9b\]: I would trust the results of performance tests.

\[C9c\]: I would trust the results of model-based performance predictions.

| Predefined Response | C9a | C9b | C9c |
| - | - | - | - |
| Strongly disagree | 0 | 0 | 2 (11.11 %) |
| Disagree | 0 | 0 | 0 |
| Slightly disagree | 1 (5.56 %) | 1 (5.56 %) | 4 (22.22 %) |
| Neutral | 3 (16.67 %) | 2 (11.11 %) | 2 (11.11 %) |
| Slightly agree | 1 (5.56 %) | 3 (16.67 %) | 6 (33.33 %) |
| Agree | 10 (55.56 %) | 10 (55.56 %) | 3 (16.67 %) |
| Strongly agree | 3 (16.67 %) | 2 (11.11 %) | 1 (5.56 %) |


| Quantile | C9a | C9b | C9c |
| - | - | - | - |
| 0 % | Slightly disagree | Slightly disagree | Strongly disagree |
| 25 % | Slightly agree | Slightly agree | Slightly disagree |
| 50 % | Agree | Agree | Slightly agree |
| 75 % | Agree | Agree | Slightly agree |
| 100 % | Strongly agree | Strongly agree | Strongly agree |

| 25 % | Neutral | Slightly agree | Neutral |
| 50 % | Slightly agree | Agree | Slightly agree |
| 75 % | Agree | Strongly agree | Agree |
| 100 % | Agree | Strongly agree | Strongly agree |

## \[C8a\] - \[C8b\]

\[C8a\]: Performance management is important in our company.

\[C8b\]: Performance management is important in our team.

| Predefined Response | C8a | C8b |
| - | - | - |
| Very unimportant | 2 (10.00 %) | 1 (5.00 %) |
| Unimportant | 1 (5.00 %) | 1 (5.00 %) |
| Neutral | 4 (20.00 %) | 3 (15.00 %) |
| Important | 9 (45.00 %) | 10 (50.00 %) |
| Very important | 4 (20.00 %) | 5 (25.00 %) |

| - | - | - |
| 0 % | Very unimportant | Very unimportant |
| 25 % | Neutral | Neutral - Important |
| 50 % | Important | Important |

| 100 % | Very important | Very important |

## \[Co2DevTimeLearn\] - \[Co2PMTimeLearn\]

\[Co2DevTimeLearn\]: How much time would you be willing to invest in setting up and learning a new performance prediction tool?

\[Co2PMTimeLearn\]: How much overall time would you be willing that people of your team invest in setting up and learning a new performance prediction tool?

| - | - | - |

| 1 working day | 0 | 1 (33.33 %) |

| 4-5 working days | 4 (36.36 %) | 0 |
| 6-10 working days | 1 (9.09 %) | 0 |
| More than 10 working days | 0 | 0 |

## \[Co2DevTimeLearn\] - \[Co2PMTimeLearn\] - \[Co3DevTimeAdoption\] - \[Co3PMTimeAdoption\]

\[Co2DevTimeLearn\]: How much time would you be willing to invest in setting up and learning a new performance prediction tool?

\[Co2PMTimeLearn\]: How much overall time would you be willing that people of your team invest in setting up and learning a new performance prediction tool?

\[Co3DevTimeAdoption\]: If a new performance prediction tool requires adoption to your specific technologies and programming languages, how much time would you be willing to invest in this adoption?

\[Co3PMTimeAdoption\]: If a new performance prediction tool requires adoption to your team's specific technologies and programming languages, how much overall time would you be willing that people of your team invest in this adoption?

| Predefined Response | Co2DevTimeLearn | Co2PMTimeLearn | Co3DevTimeAdoption | Co3PMTimeAdoption |
| - | - | - | - | - |
| Less than 1 week | 10 | 3 | 4 | 1 |
| 1-2 weeks | 1 | 0 | 3 | 1 |
| More than 2 weeks | 0 | 0 | 5 | 1 |
